## Definitions

### Pasting commuting triangles into commuting squares along homotopic diagonals

Two [commuting triangles](foundation-core.commuting-triangles-of-maps.md)

```text
   A         A --> X
  | \         \    |
  |  \ H  L  K \   |
  |   \         \  |
  v    v         v v
  B --> Y         Y
```

with a [homotopic](foundation-core.homotopies.md) diagonal may be pasted into a
commuting square

```text
  A -----> X
  |        |
  |        |
  v        v
  B -----> Y.
```

### Inverting squares horizontally and vertically

If the horizontal/vertical maps in a commuting square are both
[equivalences](foundation-core.equivalences.md), then the square remains
commuting if we invert those equivalences.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="coherence-square-inv-horizontal"></a><a id="3353" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#3353" class="Function">coherence-square-inv-horizontal</a> <a id="3385" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="3389" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3390" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#3390" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="3393" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#3393" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="3396" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#3396" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="3399" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#3399" class="Bound">l4</a> <a id="3402" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3404" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="3409" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3411" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3412" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#3412" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3414" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3416" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="3419" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#3390" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="3421" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3423" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3424" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#3424" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="3426" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3428" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="3431" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#3393" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="3433" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3435" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3436" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#3436" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="3438" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3440" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="3443" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#3396" class="Bound">l3</a><a id="3445" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3447" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3448" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#3448" class="Bound">Y</a> <a id="3450" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3452" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="3455" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#3399" class="Bound">l4</a><a id="3457" class="Symbol">}</a>

      <a id="5069" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="5071" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#4842" class="Bound">bottom</a><a id="5077" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="5085" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="5087" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#4849" class="Bound">H</a><a id="5088" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>
### Commuting squares of maps induce commuting squares of precomposition maps

Every commuting square

```text
             top
    A -----------------> X
    |                    |
    |                    |
   left       ⇗        right
    |                    |
    v                    v
    B -----------------> Y
            bottom
```

induces a commuting square of
[precomposition functions](foundation-core.precomposition-functions.md)

```text
              precomp bottom S
      (A → S) ----------------> (B → S)
        |                         |
        |                         |
 precomp right S     ⇙     precomp left S
        |                         |
        v                         v
      (X → S) ----------------> (Y → S)
                precomp top S
```

Note both that the order of composition has been flipped as well as the
direction of the homotopy.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="5990" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="5997" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#5997" class="Module">_</a>

### Commuting squares of maps induce commuting squares of postcomposition maps

Every commuting square

```text
             top
    A -----------------> X
    |                    |
    |                    |
   left       ⇗        right
    |                    |
    v                    v
    B -----------------> Y
            bottom
```

induces a commuting square of
[postcomposition functions](foundation-core.postcomposition-functions.md)

```text
              postcomp S top
     (S → A) ----------------> (S → X)
        |                         |
        |                         |
 postcomp S left     ⇗     postcomp S right
        |                         |
        v                         v
     (S → B) ----------------> (S → Y)
             postcomp S bottom
```

<pre class="Agda"><a id="7501" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="7508" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7508" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="7512" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7513" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7513" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="7516" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7516" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="7519" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7519" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="7522" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7522" class="Bound">l4</a> <a id="7525" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7525" class="Bound">l5</a> <a id="7528" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7530" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="7535" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="7539" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7540" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7540" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="7542" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7544" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="7547" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7513" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="7549" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7551" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7552" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7552" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="7554" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7556" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="7559" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7516" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="7561" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7563" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7564" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7564" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="7566" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7568" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="7571" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7519" class="Bound">l3</a><a id="7573" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7575" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7576" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7576" class="Bound">Y</a> <a id="7578" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7580" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="7583" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7522" class="Bound">l4</a><a id="7585" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="7589" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7590" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7590" class="Bound">top</a> <a id="7594" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7596" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7540" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="7598" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7600" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7564" class="Bound">X</a><a id="7601" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7603" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7604" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7604" class="Bound">left</a> <a id="7609" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7611" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7540" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="7613" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7615" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7552" class="Bound">B</a><a id="7616" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7618" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7619" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7619" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="7625" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7627" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7564" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="7629" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7631" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7576" class="Bound">Y</a><a id="7632" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7634" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7635" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7635" class="Bound">bottom</a> <a id="7642" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7644" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7552" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="7646" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7648" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7576" class="Bound">Y</a><a id="7649" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="7653" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="7662" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7662" class="Function">postcomp-coherence-square-maps</a> <a id="7693" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="7699" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7700" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7700" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="7702" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7704" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="7707" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7525" class="Bound">l5</a><a id="7709" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7711" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="7717" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#862" class="Function">coherence-square-maps</a> <a id="7739" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7590" class="Bound">top</a> <a id="7743" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7604" class="Bound">left</a> <a id="7748" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7619" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="7754" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#7635" class="Bound">bottom</a> <a id="7761" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="7767" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#862" class="Function">coherence-square-maps</a>

## Properties

### Taking vertical inversions of squares is an inverse operation

Vertical composition of a square with the square obtained by inverting the
vertical maps fits into a [prism](foundation.commuting-prisms-of-maps.md) with
the reflexivity square.

The analogous result for horizontal composition remains to be formalized.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="8582" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="8589" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#8589" class="Module">_</a>

### Associativity of vertical pasting

The proof of associativity of horizontal pasting may be found in
[`foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-maps`](foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-maps.md).

</pre>
### Naturality of commuting squares of maps with respect to identifications

Similarly to the naturality square of homotopies and
[identifications](foundation-core.identity-types.md), we have a naturality
square of coherence squares of maps and identifications:

```text
           ap f (ap g p)
  f (g x) =============== f (g y)
     ‖                       ‖
 H x ‖                       ‖ H y
     ‖                       ‖
  h (k x) =============== h (k y)
           ap h (ap k p)           .
```

<pre class="Agda"><a id="16634" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="16641" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16641" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="16645" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="16647" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16647" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="16650" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16650" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="16653" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16653" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="16656" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16656" class="Bound">l4</a> <a id="16659" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16661" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="16666" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16668" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16669" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16669" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="16671" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16673" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="16676" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16647" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="16678" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16680" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16681" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16681" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="16683" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16685" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="16688" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16650" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="16690" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16692" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16693" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16693" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="16695" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16697" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="16700" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16653" class="Bound">l3</a><a id="16702" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16704" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16705" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16705" class="Bound">D</a> <a id="16707" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16709" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="16712" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16656" class="Bound">l4</a><a id="16714" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="16718" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16720" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16720" class="Bound">top</a> <a id="16724" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16726" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16669" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="16728" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16730" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16681" class="Bound">B</a><a id="16731" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16733" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16734" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16734" class="Bound">left</a> <a id="16739" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16741" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16669" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="16743" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16745" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16693" class="Bound">C</a><a id="16746" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16748" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16749" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16749" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="16755" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16757" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16681" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="16759" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16761" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16705" class="Bound">D</a><a id="16762" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16764" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16765" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16765" class="Bound">bottom</a> <a id="16772" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16774" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16693" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="16776" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16778" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16705" class="Bound">D</a><a id="16779" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="16783" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16785" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16785" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="16787" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16789" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#862" class="Function">coherence-square-maps</a> <a id="16811" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16720" class="Bound">top</a> <a id="16815" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16734" class="Bound">left</a> <a id="16820" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16749" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="16826" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16765" class="Bound">bottom</a><a id="16832" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="16836" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="16845" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16845" class="Function">nat-coherence-square-maps</a> <a id="16871" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="16877" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="16879" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16879" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="16881" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16881" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="16883" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16885" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16669" class="Bound">A</a><a id="16886" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16888" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16889" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16889" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="16891" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16893" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16879" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="16895" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1953" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="16897" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16881" class="Bound">y</a><a id="16898" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16900" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="16906" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-identifications.html#873" class="Function">coherence-square-identifications</a>
      <a id="16945" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16947" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-functions.html#730" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="16950" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16765" class="Bound">bottom</a> <a id="16957" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16958" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-functions.html#730" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="16961" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16734" class="Bound">left</a> <a id="16966" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16889" class="Bound">p</a><a id="16967" class="Symbol">))</a>
      <a id="16976" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16978" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16785" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="16980" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16879" class="Bound">x</a><a id="16981" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="16989" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16991" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16785" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="16993" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16881" class="Bound">y</a><a id="16994" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="17002" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="17004" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-functions.html#730" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="17007" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16749" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="17013" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17014" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-functions.html#730" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="17017" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16720" class="Bound">top</a> <a id="17021" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16889" class="Bound">p</a><a id="17022" class="Symbol">))</a>
  <a id="17027" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16845" class="Function">nat-coherence-square-maps</a> <a id="17053" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1922" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="17058" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17060" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#3545" class="Function">right-unit</a>
</pre>
As a corollary, whenever we have two coherence squares touching at a vertex:

```text
  A -----> B
  |        |
  |   H ⇗  |
  V        V
  C -----> D -----> X
           |        |
           |   K ⇗  |
           V        V
           Y -----> Z ,
```

there is a homotopy between first applying `H`, then `K`, and first applying
`K`, then `H`.

  <a id="18039" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#17844" class="Function">swap-nat-coherence-square-maps</a> <a id="18070" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#18070" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18072" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="18078" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#16845" class="Function">nat-coherence-square-maps</a> <a id="18104" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#17638" class="Bound">mid-right</a> <a id="18114" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#17658" class="Bound">mid-bottom</a> <a id="18125" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#17679" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="18131" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#17695" class="Bound">bottom</a> <a id="18138" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#17772" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="18140" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18141" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#17715" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="18143" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#18070" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18144" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### Commutativity of horizontal and vertical pasting

Given a square of commuting squares, like so:

```text
  A -----> B -----> C
  |        |        |
  |    ⇗   |    ⇗   |
  V        V        V
  X -----> Y -----> Z
  |        |        |
  |    ⇗   |    ⇗   |
  V        V        V
  M -----> N -----> O ,
```

we have two choices for obtaining the outer commuting square — either by first
vertically composing the smaller squares, and then horizontally composing the
newly created rectangles, or by first horizontally composing the squares, and
then vertically composing the rectangles.

The following lemma states that the big squares obtained by these two
compositions are again homotopic. Diagramatically, we have

```text
 H | K   H | K
 ----- ~ --|--
 L | T   L | T .
```

<pre class="Agda"><a id="18941" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="18948" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#18948" class="Module">_</a>

            <a id="21698" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="21700" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#19108" class="Bound">top-left</a><a id="21708" class="Symbol">)</a>

            <a id="22085" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="22087" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#19229" class="Bound">mid-right</a> <a id="22097" href="foundation-core.whiskering-homotopies.html#1637" class="Function Operator">·l</a> <a id="22100" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#19369" class="Bound">sq-left-top</a><a id="22111" class="Symbol">)</a>
            <a id="22125" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="22127" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#19445" class="Bound">sq-right-top</a> <a id="22140" href="foundation-core.whiskering-homotopies.html#1992" class="Function Operator">·r</a> <a id="22143" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#19108" class="Bound">top-left</a><a id="22151" class="Symbol">))))</a>
</pre>
### Distributivity of pasting squares and transposing by precomposition

Given two commuting squares which can be composed horizontally (vertically), we
know that composing them and then transposing them by precomposition gives a
homotopy that is homotopic to first transposing the squares and then composing
them.

```text
      tl       tr                tr ∘ tl
  A -----> B -----> C         A --------> C
  |        |        |         |           |
l |       m|        | r  ↦   l|          r|
  |   H    |   K    |         |   H | K   |
  v        v        v         v           v
  X -----> Y -----> Z         X --------> Z
      bl       br                br ∘ bl

         -                          -
         |                          |
         v                          v

           -∘r
    W^Z ------> W^C
     |           |
-∘br |    W^K    | -∘tr           W^(H | K)
     |           |
     v     -∘m   v                   ~
    W^Y ------> W^B   |->
     |           |                  W^K
-∘bl |    W^H    | -∘tl             ---
     |           |                  W^H
     v           v
    W^X ------> W^A
          -∘l
```

          <a id="27807" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="27809" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27810" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#27276" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="27812" href="foundation-core.whiskering-homotopies.html#1637" class="Function Operator">·l</a> <a id="27815" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#27267" class="Bound">K</a><a id="27816" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="27818" href="foundation-core.whiskering-homotopies.html#1992" class="Function Operator">·r</a> <a id="27821" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#27158" class="Bound">left-top</a><a id="27829" class="Symbol">)</a>
          <a id="27841" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="27843" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#27276" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="27845" href="foundation-core.whiskering-homotopies.html#1637" class="Function Operator">·l</a> <a id="27848" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27849" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#27224" class="Bound">right-bottom</a> <a id="27862" href="foundation-core.whiskering-homotopies.html#1637" class="Function Operator">·l</a> <a id="27865" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#27258" class="Bound">H</a><a id="27866" class="Symbol">))</a>
      <a id="27875" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#6081" class="Function">＝</a> <a id="27877" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-functions.html#730" class="Function">ap</a>

          <a id="27922" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="27924" href="foundation.precomposition-functions.html#1488" class="Function">htpy-precomp</a> <a id="27937" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#27267" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="27939" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#23437" class="Bound">W</a> <a id="27941" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#27276" class="Bound">h</a><a id="27942" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="27944" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2902" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
        <a id="27954" href="foundation-core.function-extensionality.html#3024" class="Function">eq-htpy</a>
          <a id="27972" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="27974" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27975" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#27276" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="27977" href="foundation-core.function-types.html#455" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="27979" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#27224" class="Bound">right-bottom</a><a id="27991" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="27993" href="foundation-core.whiskering-homotopies.html#1637" class="Function Operator">·l</a> <a id="27996" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#27258" class="Bound">H</a><a id="27997" class="Symbol">)</a>

          <a id="28073" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28075" href="foundation.whiskering-homotopies.html#2227" class="Function">compute-eq-htpy-right-whisk</a> <a id="28103" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#27158" class="Bound">left-top</a> <a id="28112" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28113" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#27276" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="28115" href="foundation-core.whiskering-homotopies.html#1637" class="Function Operator">·l</a> <a id="28118" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#27267" class="Bound">K</a><a id="28119" class="Symbol">))</a>
          <a id="28132" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28134" href="foundation-core.function-extensionality.html#3024" class="Function">eq-htpy</a> <a id="28142" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28143" href="foundation-core.whiskering-homotopies.html#5448" class="Function">associative-left-whisk-comp</a> <a id="28171" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#27276" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="28173" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#27224" class="Bound">right-bottom</a> <a id="28186" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#27258" class="Bound">H</a><a id="28187" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>
### Transposing by precomposition of whiskered squares

Taking a square of the form

```text
      f        top
  X -----> A -----> B
           |        |
      left |   H    | right
           v        v
           C -----> D
             bottom
```

and transposing it by precomposition results in the square

```text
  W^D -----> W^B
   |          |
   |   W^H    |
   v          v   -∘f
  W^C -----> W^A -----> W^X
```

This fact can be written as distribution of right whiskering over transposition:
`W^(H ·r f) = W^f ·l W^H`.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="28737" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="28744" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#28744" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="28748" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="28750" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#28750" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="28753" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#28753" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="28756" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#28756" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="28759" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#28759" class="Bound">l4</a> <a id="28762" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#28762" class="Bound">l5</a> <a id="28765" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#28765" class="Bound">l6</a> <a id="28768" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28770" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="28775" class="Symbol">}</a>

  <a id="28981" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#28981" class="Function">distributive-precomp-right-whisk-coherence-square-maps</a> <a id="29036" class="Symbol">:</a>

  <a id="29278" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#28981" class="Function">distributive-precomp-right-whisk-coherence-square-maps</a> <a id="29333" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#29333" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="29335" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#29335" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="29337" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="29343" href="foundation.whiskering-homotopies.html#2227" class="Function">compute-eq-htpy-right-whisk</a> <a id="29371" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#29333" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="29373" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29374" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#29335" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="29376" href="foundation-core.whiskering-homotopies.html#1637" class="Function Operator">·l</a> <a id="29379" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#28921" class="Bound">H</a><a id="29380" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
Similarly, we can calculate transpositions of left-whiskered squares with the
formula `W^(f ·l H) = W^H ·r W^f`.

<pre class="Agda">  <a id="29511" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#29511" class="Function">distributive-precomp-left-whisk-coherence-square-maps</a> <a id="29565" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="29571" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29573" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#29573" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="29575" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="29577" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#28817" class="Bound">D</a> <a id="29579" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="29581" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#28829" class="Bound">X</a><a id="29582" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="29584" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="29590" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#6151" class="Function">precomp-coherence-square-maps</a>
      <a id="29626" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29628" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#28856" class="Bound">top</a><a id="29631" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="29639" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29641" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#28870" class="Bound">left</a><a id="29645" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="29653" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29655" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#29573" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="29657" href="foundation-core.function-types.html#455" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="29659" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#28885" class="Bound">right</a><a id="29664" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="29672" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29674" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#29573" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="29676" href="foundation-core.function-types.html#455" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="29678" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#28901" class="Bound">bottom</a><a id="29684" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="29692" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29694" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#29573" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="29696" href="foundation-core.whiskering-homotopies.html#1637" class="Function Operator">·l</a> <a id="29699" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#28921" class="Bound">H</a><a id="29700" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="29708" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29710" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#28841" class="Bound">W</a><a id="29711" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="29713" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2717" class="Function Operator">~</a>
    <a id="29719" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29721" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29723" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#6151" class="Function">precomp-coherence-square-maps</a> <a id="29753" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#28856" class="Bound">top</a> <a id="29757" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#28870" class="Bound">left</a> <a id="29762" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#28885" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="29768" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#28901" class="Bound">bottom</a> <a id="29775" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#28921" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="29777" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#28841" class="Bound">W</a><a id="29778" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="29780" href="foundation-core.whiskering-homotopies.html#1992" class="Function Operator">·r</a>

  <a id="29807" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#29511" class="Function">distributive-precomp-left-whisk-coherence-square-maps</a> <a id="29861" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#29861" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="29863" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#29863" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="29865" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="29871" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-functions.html#730" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="29874" href="foundation-core.function-extensionality.html#3024" class="Function">eq-htpy</a> <a id="29882" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29883" href="foundation-core.function-extensionality.html#3024" class="Function">eq-htpy</a> <a id="29891" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="29894" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#29894" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="29896" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="29898" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#3206" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="29902" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29903" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-functions.html#1124" class="Function">ap-comp</a> <a id="29911" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#29863" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="29913" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#29861" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="29915" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29916" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#28921" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="29918" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#29894" class="Bound">a</a><a id="29919" class="Symbol">))))</a>
</pre>
### The square of function spaces induced by a composition of triangles is homotopic to the composition of induced triangles of function spaces

<pre class="Agda"><a id="30082" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="30089" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#30089" class="Module">_</a>
